Ticket: PFT-6857
Issue id: 197255
Module: Behaviour
Summary: Detention Set-up
Role: Data Officer
Source: Sheet1 - Row 62
Comment: Hello,

 Currently in Arbor detentions are unable to run at the same time with an escalation policy. This means that, for example, we have two detentions that run every single day, and our escalation system does not allow them to be escalated from one detention to the next. If a student in our school receives a Level 3 negative, they are assigned an academy detention. However, if they are assigned another level 3 negative in the same day they should be escalated to a leadership detention. They way we have been able t do this is to mark detentions run at different times, but this is not a true representation of the times of the detention and causes further admin work in terms of communications to parents and staff. My idea is a way where arbor could implement a system where students are able to be removed automatically from one detention and added to the next if the escalation process allows this. This follows on from another idea I have presented regarding detention escalation. I think it would be highly beneficial if Arbor would allow detentions to run at the same times and overlap but students still be added to the correct detention and removed from the other one to make a smooth transition for staff when handling and issuing detentions.

 I hope you understand my idea and if you have any further queries regarding this, please feel free to contact me.

Comment: I know I have sent this request in multiple times but it really is one of the most painful processes for us and our parents, so I'm going to keep suggesting it.

 If you could add a feature when setting up a trip for additional tick boxes, it would be a game changer!

 All we request is when setting up the trip, you include addition check boxes we can include if required so parents must make a selection when consenting to the trip. They could be freeform with just Yes/No answers or pre-populated with the most common questions, example:

 1) Pack Lunch Required - Do you require a SCHOOL packed lunch?

 2) Parent Volunteers Required - Are you able to volunteer?

 3) Dismissal after normal school day - Do you consent to your child being dismissed from school without collection?

 At least one of these additional questions are needed by all schools for probably 8 out of 10 trips. Question 2 would be most used by primary schools, and question 3 largely by secondary but also for primary schools if the trip is for Y5s or Y6s.

 Since moving payments over to Arbor, this has been the area that has been difficult to manage, not wanting to revert back to paper forms, we have to create a Google form to be sent out alongside the trip information for parents to answer these questions. It becomes a cumbersome process for both us and parents.

 I feel your development team could come up with ideas to have these additional boxes incorporated as Arbor has so many features in other areas of the system and would be inline with all other school payment systems who already have this feature.

 Pretty please could it be included in the roadmap :)

 There is all sorts of frustrating logic around changing submission statuses which stops you changing from certain states to others. I can think of no sensible reason why these limitations are in place. I should be trusted to change my assignment submission statuses as I see fit, rather than being arbitrarily blocked from performing certain state changes: e.g., you cannot change from 'extended' to 'not submitted', you cannot change from 'submitted late' to 'submitted', you cannot change from 'Submitted - requires marking' to 'Not submitted'.

 The entire user experience of assignments is frustrating and I am shocked it passed any kind of QA.

Ticket: PFT-6494
Issue id: 195922
Module: Attendance
Summary: Attendance Data On Arbor MAT site
Role: Head of Data and Analytics
Source: Sheet1 - Row 425
Comment: Hello,

 There are a number of points I would like to raise around attendance on the Arbor MAT site. Currently, the whole academic year attendance percentages for secondary schools are inaccurate, as they include year 11 sessions after the summer term half term, which the DfE exclude from their attendance data, so could this be looked at please to bring in line with the way DfE calculate attendance?

 Also, I would be so happy if the Arbor attendance data could somehow match the DfE figures. For example, I think the DfE data only includes students who have been on roll for a certain number of sessions, while i think Arbor includes everyone. It would just be so nice to reconcile figures, like when I look at the DfE statistical publication and it shows a % attendance figure for the 23/24 academic year, it would be so nice to run a report in Arbor and see the same figure. I know this is a lot to do and get right, but wouldn't it be amazing if we could achieve this and see the same figures. I also know that staff can probably make retrospective historical amendments to Arbor, which is why the stats may not reconcile, but it would be amazing if they could. Or, would it be possible to build into Arbor stats from past DfE publications, this would make dashboard creation even easier, as currently I go away and pull out the historical stats from Analyse school performance or the DfE statistical releases. Having these available on Arbor would make things easier.

 In the MAT Arbor MIS, when I navigate to Analytics -> Attendance and then click on the box for statutory attendance a graph appears showing attendance for this academic year by phase. However, this compares the attendance up to today for this year with the attendance in the whole of last academic year. This is good, but of course the secondary data for last year is inaccurate, as it includes the year 11 data after the summer half term, but what I would really like to see is an toggle option for comparing 1. the attendance % for this academic year up to this point with the corresponding period last year, or 2. for the whole of last year.

 On the MAT MIS site and also school sites, attendance breakdowns by characteristics are shown, so we have No SEN attendance vs SEN attendance. However, what would be really helpful is to also break this down further by SEN provision, so attendance by SEN K code vs attendance by SEN E code. This additional breakdown is available for suspensions on the MAT site, but not for attendance currently.

 One of the things I would find so helpful is if the attendance sessions without a mark on Arbor were flagged up somewhere in a report. For example, if I build a custom report I can ask for specific attendance codes like /, \, N, M, S etc, but I can't return any sessions which are missing codes. So these are the sessions which don't have a mark. Also, I can only return the attendance codes from the custom reports which are currently used by the DfE, but it may well be that some academies may have used old codes like the old holiday agreed code or a Covid reason for absence. I think the system still allows for entry of these old codes unless I am mistaken, so I need a way of checking to see if academies have used these, along for easily checking on sessions with missing codes. I know I could use Power BI, but I would find it so helpful if this were built into an Arbor custom report.

 In the school Arbor sites, the Students -> Attendance -> Statistics is a brilliant feature. However, in the wonderful filter menu, I don't believe there is an option to view attendance by day of the week. For example, to see Friday attendance quick for the year quickly in here. This would be a helpful addition.

 Thank you,

 Ian

Ticket: PFT-6472
Issue id: 195839
Module: Medical
Summary: Allow us to report on Medical Notes
Role: MIS Assistant
Source: Sheet1 - Row 447
Comment: We noticed that pastoral managers were adding medical conditions and dietary requirements as pinned pastoral notes. I looked into this by reporting on all pastoral notes and manually highlighting the ones i intended to change to medical. some were easy and very obviously medical conditions eg. asthma, epilepsy, allergies, etc so i created these as medical conditions and/or dietary requirements instead. however there were things that arent quite named defined medical conditions but i would describe more as a medical note than a pastoral note - e.g. legs hurt after exercise, can get headaches after screen use, can be prone to fainting. etc. so i went through and added these as medical notes and deleted the pastoral note. however, i then realised you *cannot report on medical notes*. why is this? this means that if a teacher is taking children on a trip and wants to pull all medical info, they would miss important medical information like this if they are a medical note not medical condition. so for example the girl we have that is prone to fainting, she hasn't got a named defined medical condition for this so therefore this shouldn't be flagged as a condition but should still be recorded under medical and would *definitely* be relevant when taking children on trips.

 the current workaround would be to either: artificially inflate the number of medical conditions in school by recording everything medical or health related as a 'Medical _condition ' which I don't think is accurate or right. Other than this, I could record them as pastoral notes and write the word 'medical' as the summary to allow this to be reportable/filterable but again this seems incorrect and strange as it's not a pastoral issue it's a medical one.

 the overall reason that this should be added is related to safeguarding; it's critical that staff can easily access medical information for a cohort whenever they need to so im worried that currently important medical info could be missed when reporting on this. if we could add an additional field when reporting ABOUT STUDENTS, so you could do Student Name, DOB, class, medical conditions, medical NOTES, contact details.

 this would mean anything relevant and medical related could all be seen in one place.

 Thank you for reading, i sincerely hope this can be actioned.

 Mrs Trotter, your idea of having planned absence notes that remain linked to attendance records and certificates but are concealed by default on the class register with just a discreet indicator sounds very practical.  The steps I take to send truancy calls are as follows.

 Firstly, I send truancy calls about 10 and 10:30AM after Period 2.

 1. Students.

 2. Attendance.

 3. Absentees.

 4. Absentees by date.

 5. Lessons and filters with only N codes.

 6. Marks and filter N codes only.

 If a student has a present [one period] code for/of one of the 2 Periods, should not appear on the list of absent list.

 This is how Arbor used to operate which I was happy with.

 Nowadays; Abor is including some students on the absent list who are in School and present to truancy call list which is then sent home and parents get angry because their child is in School but they got truancy calls.

 What I am wishing for, is that Arbor should eliminate all students with a present mark and leave only students with double N codes. Not with one present and one absent.

 Please check again for me. I know Arbor used to be so accurate in the past 2 years but from about May onwards, it is causing me problems from parents who don't realise that I am not even the one who marks students.

 I look forward to hearing from you once again.

 Kind regards

 Persis Katto-Nagel

For example the overall behaviour could be 'Discrimination' and then within that, staff pick from a drop-down of the type of discrimination.  We would also like to use behaviour incidents to track when students are trained on different Tech equipment. This should work well as behaviour incidents are reportable, tied to a date and staff member, so would provide the schools with exactly what they want (they want to know when a student has been trained on a particular type of equipment and with which staff member). However, the downside of this is that currently we will have to add one overarching behaviour incident type, 'DT Equipment Training' for example, then rely on teachers filling in the narrative with the equipment name e.g. drill, hand saw, etc. However, if we want to use a live feed to report on this in excel for example, or even within Arbor, filtering etc will be a nightmare as the field is free text so teachers will all write these things differently. We don't want to have 20+ behaviour types in the list that are just DT tools as this will completely clog the behaviour field. Therefore it would be great to have sub-categories, so we could allow teachers to pick DT Equipment Training and then use the pre-defined drop-down fields to select the specific tool, NOT opening this up to free text.
